\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \ \ \ \ std::string::size\_type\ end\ =\ s.find(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}::"{}},\ strlen(prefix));}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (end\ !=\ s.npos)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Erase\ everything\ between\ the\ initial\ \`{}std`\ and\ the\ second\ \`{}::`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \ \ \ \ \ \ s.erase(strlen(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}std"{}}),\ end\ -\/\ strlen(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}std"{}}));}

\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \}}
